JSON.parse(data) : [];\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error(\'Error reading from storage:\', error);\n      return [];\n    }\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get a single item by ID\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} id - Item ID\n   * @returns {object|null} Item or null if not found\n   */\n  getById(key, id) {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    return items.find(item => item.id === id) || null;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Update an item\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} id - Item ID\n   * @param {object} updates - Updates to apply\n   * @returns {object|null} Updated item or null if not found\n   */\n  update(key, id, updates) {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    const index = items.findIndex(item => item.id === id);\n    \n    if (index === -1) return null;\n    \n    items[index] = {\n      ...items[index],\n      ...updates,\n      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()\n    };\n    \n    localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));\n    return items[index];\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Delete an item\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} id - Item ID\n   * @returns {boolean} Success status\n   */\n  delete(key, id) {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    const filtered = items.filter(item => item.id !== id);\n    \n    if (filtered.length === items.length) return false;\n    \n    localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(filtered));\n    return true;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Search items by query\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} query - Search query\n   * @returns {array} Matching items\n   */\n  search(key, query) {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    const lowerQuery = query.toLowerCase();\n    \n    return items.filter(item => {\n      return Object.values(item).some(value => {\n        if (typeof value === \'string\') {\n          return value.toLowerCase().includes(lowerQuery);\n        }\n        return false;\n      });\n    });\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Filter items by criteria\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {function} predicate - Filter function\n   * @returns {array} Filtered items\n   */\n  filter(key, predicate) {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    return items.filter(predicate);\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Sort items\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} field - Field to sort by\n   * @param {string} order - \'asc\' or \'desc\'\n   * @returns {array} Sorted items\n   */\n  sort(key, field, order = \'desc\') {\n    const items = this.getAll(key);\n    return items.sort((a, b) => {\n      const aVal = a[field];\n      const bVal = b[field];\n      \n      if (order === \'asc\') {\n        return aVal > bVal ? 1 : -1;\n      } else {\n        return aVal < bVal ? 1 : -1;\n      }\n    });\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get recent items\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {number} limit - Number of items to return\n   * @returns {array} Recent items\n   */\n  getRecent(key, limit = 10) {\n    const items = this.sort(key, \'timestamp\', \'desc\');\n    return items.slice(0, limit);\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Link items together\n   * @param {string} sourceKey - Source storage key\n   * @param {string} sourceId - Source item ID\n   * @param {string} targetKey - Target storage key\n   * @param {string} targetId - Target item ID\n   * @returns {boolean} Success status\n   */\n  link(sourceKey, sourceId, targetKey, targetId) {\n    const sourceItem = this.getById(sourceKey, sourceId);\n    if (!sourceItem) return false;\n    \n    if (!sourceItem.links) {\n      sourceItem.links = [];\n    }\n    \n    sourceItem.links.push({\n      key: targetKey,\n      id: targetId,\n      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n    });\n    \n    return this.update(sourceKey, sourceId, { links: sourceItem.links }) !== null;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get linked items\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} id - Item ID\n   * @returns {array} Linked items\n   */\n  getLinked(key, id) {\n    const item = this.getById(key, id);\n    if (!item || !item.links) return [];\n    \n    return item.links.map(link => {\n      const linkedItem = this.getById(link.key, link.id);\n      return linkedItem ? { ...linkedItem, linkType: link.key } : null;\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Add tags to an item\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} id - Item ID\n   * @param {array} tags - Tags to add\n   * @returns {boolean} Success status\n   */\n  addTags(key, id, tags) {\n    const item = this.getById(key, id);\n    if (!item) return false;\n    \n    const currentTags = item.tags || [];\n    const newTags = [...new Set([...currentTags, ...tags])];\n    \n    return this.update(key, id, { tags: newTags }) !== null;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get items by tag\n   * @param {string} key - Storage key\n   * @param {string} tag - Tag to filter by\n   * @returns {array} Items with the tag\n   */\n  getByTag(key, tag) {\n    return this.filter(key, item => {\n      return item.tags && item.tags.includes(tag);\n    });\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Export all data\n   * @returns {object} All storage data\n   */\n  exportAll() {\n    const data = {};\n    Object.entries(this.KEYS).forEach(([name, key]) => {\n      data[name] = this.getAll(key);\n    });\n    return data;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Import data\n   * @param {object} data - Data to import\n   * @param {boolean} merge - Whether to merge with existing data\n   * @returns {boolean} Success status\n   */\n  importData(data, merge = false) {\n    try {\n      Object.entries(data).forEach(([name, items]) => {\n        const key = this.KEYS[name];\n        if (!key) return;\n        \n        if (merge) {\n          const existing = this.getAll(key);\n          const merged = [...existing, ...items];\n          localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(merged));\n        } else {\n          localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));\n        }\n      });\n      return true;\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error(\'Error importing data:\', error);\n      return false;\n    }\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Clear all data\n   * @param {string} key - Optional specific key to clear\n   */\n  clear(key = null) {\n    if (key) {\n      localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify([]));\n    } else {\n      Object.values(this.KEYS).forEach(k => {\n        localStorage.setItem(k, JSON.stringify([]));\n      });\n    }\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get storage statistics\n   * @returns {object} Storage stats\n   */\n  getStats() {\n    const stats = {};\n    Object.entries(this.KEYS).forEach(([name, key]) => {\n      const items = this.getAll(key);\n      stats[name] = {\n        count: items.length,\n        size: new Blob([JSON.stringify(items)]).size\n      };\n    });\n    \n    const totalSize = Object.values(stats).reduce((sum, stat) => sum + stat.size, 0);\n    const totalCount = Object.values(stats).reduce((sum, stat) => sum + stat.count, 0);\n    \n    return {\n      ...stats,\n      total: {\n        count: totalCount,\n        size: totalSize,\n        sizeFormatted: this.formatBytes(totalSize)\n      }\n    };\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Check if export is unlocked\n   * @returns {boolean} Export unlock status\n   */\n  isExportUnlocked() {\n    return localStorage.getItem(this.KEYS.EXPORT_UNLOCKED) === \'true\';\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Unlock export feature\n   */\n  unlockExport() {\n    localStorage.setItem(this.KEYS.EXPORT_UNLOCKED, \'true\');\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Get or set preferences\n   * @param {object} updates - Optional updates to apply\n   * @returns {object} Current preferences\n   */\n  preferences(updates = null) {\n    const current = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.KEYS.PREFERENCES) || \'{}\');\n    \n    if (updates) {\n      const updated = { ...current, ...updates };\n      localStorage.setItem(this.KEYS.PREFERENCES, JSON.stringify(updated));\n      return updated;\n    }\n    \n    return current;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Generate unique ID\n   * @returns {string} Unique ID\n   */\n  generateId() {\n    return `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;\n  },\n\n  /**\n   * Format bytes to human readable\n   * @param {number} bytes - Bytes to format\n   * @returns {string} Formatted string\n   */\n  formatBytes(bytes) {\n    if (bytes === 0) return \'0 Bytes\';\n    const k = 1024;\n    const sizes = [\'Bytes\', \'KB\', \'MB\', \'GB\'];\n    const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));\n    return Math.round(bytes / Math.pow(k, i) * 100) / 100 + \' \' + sizes[i];\n  }\n};\n\n// Initialize storage on load\nif (typeof window !== \'undefined\') {\n  QuantumStorage.init();\n}\n\n// Export for use in modules\nif (typeof module !== \'undefined\' && module.exports) {\n  module.exports = QuantumStorage;\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

\'Connect with universe\'\n  }\n};\n```\n\n#### Playlist Player Class\n```javascript\nclass PlaylistPlayer {\n  constructor() {\n    this.audioContext = null;\n    this.currentPlaylist = null;\n    this.currentStep = 0;\n    this.isPlaying = false;\n    this.isPaused = false;\n    this.startTime = 0;\n    this.pauseTime = 0;\n    this.oscillators = [];\n    this.gainNodes = [];\n    this.masterGain = null;\n    this.analyser = null;\n    this.progressInterval = null;\n    this.transitionTimeout = null;\n  }\n  \n  async loadPlaylist(playlistId) {\n    this.currentPlaylist = playlistLibrary[playlistId];\n    if (!this.currentPlaylist) {\n      throw new Error(\'Playlist not found\');\n    }\n    \n    // Prepare playlist data\n    this.currentStep = 0;\n    this.isPlaying = false;\n    this.isPaused = false;\n    \n    return this.currentPlaylist;\n  }\n  \n  async play() {\n    if (this.isPlaying) return;\n    \n    // Initialize audio context\n    this.audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();\n    \n    // Create master gain\n    this.masterGain = this.audioContext.createGain();\n    this.masterGain.gain.value = 0.7;\n    \n    // Create analyser\n    this.analyser = this.audioContext.createAnalyser();\n    this.analyser.fftSize = 2048;\n    \n    // Connect chain\n    this.masterGain.connect(this.analyser);\n    this.analyser.connect(this.audioContext.destination);\n    \n    this.isPlaying = true;\n    this.startTime = Date.now();\n    \n    // Start first step\n    await this.playStep(0);\n    \n    // Start progress tracking\n    this.startProgressTracking();\n    \n    // Update UI\n    this.updateUI();\n  }\n  \n  async playStep(stepIndex) {\n    if (stepIndex >= this.currentPlaylist.sequence.length) {\n      // Playlist complete\n      this.onPlaylistComplete();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    this.currentStep = stepIndex;\n    const step = this.currentPlaylist.sequence[stepIndex];\n    \n    // Show step info\n    this.showStepInfo(step);\n    \n    // Create oscillator for this step\n    const oscillator = this.audioContext.createOscillator();\n    oscillator.type = step.waveform || \'sine\';\n    oscillator.frequency.value = step.frequency;\n    \n    // Create gain node for fade in/out\n    const gainNode = this.audioContext.createGain();\n    gainNode.gain.value = 0;\n    \n    // Connect\n    oscillator.connect(gainNode);\n    gainNode.connect(this.masterGain);\n    \n    // Store references\n    this.oscillators.push(oscillator);\n    this.gainNodes.push(gainNode);\n    \n    // Start oscillator\n    oscillator.start();\n    \n    // Fade in\n    const fadeInDuration = step.fadeIn || 30;\n    gainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(\n      step.volume || 0.7,\n      this.audioContext.currentTime + fadeInDuration\n    );\n    \n    // Add binaural if enabled\n    if (step.binaural && step.binaural.enabled) {\n      this.addBinauralBeat(step.frequency, step.binaural.beat, gainNode);\n    }\n    \n    // Add isochronic if enabled\n    if (step.isochronic && step.isochronic.enabled) {\n      this.addIsochronicTone(step.frequency, step.isochronic.rate, gainNode);\n    }\n    \n    // Schedule fade out and next step\n    const fadeOutDuration = step.fadeOut || 30;\n    const stepDuration = step.duration;\n    \n    this.transitionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {\n      // Fade out current step\n      gainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(\n        0,\n        this.audioContext.currentTime + fadeOutDuration\n      );\n      \n      // Start next step after fade out\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        oscillator.stop();\n        this.playStep(stepIndex + 1);\n      }, fadeOutDuration * 1000);\n      \n    }, (stepDuration - fadeOutDuration) * 1000);\n  }\n  \n  addBinauralBeat(baseFreq, beatFreq, targetGain) {\n    // Create left and right oscillators\n    const leftPanner = this.audioContext.createStereoPanner();\n    leftPanner.pan.value = -1;\n    leftPanner.connect(targetGain);\n    \n    const rightPanner = this.audioContext.createStereoPanner();\n    rightPanner.pan.value = 1;\n    rightPanner.connect(targetGain);\n    \n    const leftOsc = this.audioContext.createOscillator();\n    leftOsc.frequency.value = baseFreq;\n    leftOsc.connect(leftPanner);\n    leftOsc.start();\n    \n    const rightOsc = this.audioContext.createOscillator();\n    rightOsc.frequency.value = baseFreq + beatFreq;\n    rightOsc.connect(rightPanner);\n    rightOsc.start();\n    \n    this.oscillators.push(leftOsc, rightOsc);\n  }\n  \n  addIsochronicTone(baseFreq, pulseRate, targetGain) {\n    //
